\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Accelerometer full-\/scale management between UI chain and OIS chain. When XL UI is on, the full scale is the same between UI/\+OIS and is chosen by the UI CTRL registers; when XL UI is in PD, the OIS can choose the FS. Full scales are independent between the UI/\+OIS chain but both bound to 8 g.\mbox{[}set\mbox{]}. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
int32\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{group__LSM6DSOX___ga859b9aab4caba6044560776e4f5bfd17}{lsm6dsox\+\_\+aux\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+get}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{structstmdev__ctx__t}{stmdev\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}ctx, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__LSM6DSOX_gab25741f38ab728495091807aec7f44fb}{lsm6dsox\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}val)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Accelerometer full-\/scale management between UI chain and OIS chain. \Hypertarget{group__LSM6DSOX___ga859b9aab4caba6044560776e4f5bfd17}\label{group__LSM6DSOX___ga859b9aab4caba6044560776e4f5bfd17} 
\index{Auxiliary\_interface@{Auxiliary\_interface}!lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get@{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get}}
\index{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get@{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get}!Auxiliary\_interface@{Auxiliary\_interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get()}{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t lsm6dsox\+\_\+aux\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structstmdev__ctx__t}{stmdev\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__LSM6DSOX_gab25741f38ab728495091807aec7f44fb}{lsm6dsox\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accelerometer full-\/scale management between UI chain and OIS chain. When XL UI is on, the full scale is the same between UI/\+OIS and is chosen by the UI CTRL registers; when XL UI is in PD, the OIS can choose the FS. Full scales are independent between the UI/\+OIS chain but both bound to 8 g.\mbox{[}get\mbox{]}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & read / write interface definitions \\
\hline
{\em val} & Get the values of xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode in reg CTRL8\+\_\+\+XL \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em interface} & status (MANDATORY\+: return 0 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} no Error) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{Auxiliary\_interface@{Auxiliary\_interface}!lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set@{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set}}
\index{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set@{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set}!Auxiliary\_interface@{Auxiliary\_interface}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set()}{lsm6dsox\_aux\_xl\_fs\_mode\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t lsm6dsox\+\_\+aux\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structstmdev__ctx__t}{stmdev\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{ctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__LSM6DSOX_gab25741f38ab728495091807aec7f44fb}{lsm6dsox\+\_\+xl\+\_\+fs\+\_\+mode\+\_\+t}}}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Accelerometer full-\/scale management between UI chain and OIS chain. When XL UI is on, the full scale is the same between UI/\+OIS and is chosen by the UI CTRL registers; when XL UI is in PD, the OIS can choose the FS. Full scales are independent between the UI/\+OIS chain but both bound to 8 g.\mbox{[}set\mbox{]}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
